      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-6110cc5f4828f94c0f607b07"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868257209_308"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868257209_307"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-dbbd5ca122cada2c1e30"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0947368s;"><strong>Nestled in the residential area of Sengkang West and located within the vicinity of Sengkang Methodist Church, Sengkang Methodist&nbsp; Preschool offers a spacious, safe and conducive environment with both indoor and large outdoor spaces that are purposefully designed and equipped to support children’s holistic development and play-and-inquiry-based learning.</strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0986842s;"><strong>We were established in 2003 and attract a unique mix of children from diverse nationalities and cultural backgrounds. Students benefit from the exposure to and close interaction with peers in the rich atmosphere of diversity. Our strong team of qualified and experienced principal and teachers are well-trained to administer our broad-based curriculum to attain our desired learning outcomes as well as inculcate our core values and nurture positive learning dispositions in our children. </strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.102632s;"><strong>We offer 4-hour to 6-hour pre-nursery, nursery and kindergarten programmes with a holistic STEM-based and tech-enabled curriculum that nurtures every child to be a person of Good Character, who is an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur. </strong></p><p style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.106579s;" class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true"></p>
</div>

  <p class="preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.114474s;"></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.118421s;"><strong>Sengkang Methodist Preschool&nbsp;is SPARK-Certified.</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block markdown-block sqs-block-markdown" data-block-type="44" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1630209167580_8287"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.122368s;"><span data-preserve-html-node="true" class="readMore">Read More</span></p>
<p class="show preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.126316s;">SPARK certification is a mark of quality by the Early Childhood Development Agency (ECDA) for processes and practices that lead to the desired outcomes of preschool education based on eagerness to learn, holistic development and child’s well-being.</p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.134211s;"><strong>Sengkang Methodist Preschool is accredited as Healthy Pre-School (Platinum).</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block markdown-block sqs-block-markdown" data-block-type="44" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1630209167580_11235"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.138158s;"><span data-preserve-html-node="true" class="readMore">Read More</span></p>
<p class="show preFade fadeIn" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.142105s;">Healthy Preschool (Platinum) is an accreditation by Singapore's Health Promotion Board(HPB). In line with our belief that a healthy school contributes to better health and education outcomes, we have implemented health promotion practices (in the areas of supportive environment, targeted intervention and capacity building) for our preschoolers and staff in support of comprehensive and holistic health for all. </p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.189474s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><em>Principal’s Message </em></h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.193421s;"><strong>Ms Joanne Low</strong></p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.197368s;">Sengkang Methodist Preschool’s mission is to create opportunities for our students to be adventurous explorers to try out things that they have never done before. All the learning activities are planned to lead children to take up the challenge to explore the unknown, and the resilience to persevere from failure to success.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.201316s;">Our curriculum integrates Christian values for the children to learn, trust, obey and be humble. It equips them with the ability to contribute to the community, create changes or improve on existing structures and make things happen through actions and words.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.205263s;"></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.292105s;"><strong>One of the programmes we have included in our curriculum is the KidzLive : I Can Protect Myself&nbsp; programme launched by Children’s Society since 2011 to educate and empower children on self-protection. Through the programme, our children learn body-safety skills which is key to preventing child sexual abuse. </strong></p>

</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--community-initiatives-" id="tab--community-initiatives-" href="#tabpanel--community-initiatives-" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a490c7244840303583aaf/1628064012412/Group+67.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Community Initiatives 
</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--community-initiatives-" id="tabpanel--community-initiatives-" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-905d81c8775d31cee7ec"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.296053s;"><strong>Participation in community initiatives like the Start Small, Dream Big project provides opportunities for our children to put the values that they learn in our daily curriculum to meaningful and authentic action.</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel-learning-journeys-" id="tab-learning-journeys-" href="#tabpanel-learning-journeys-" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a4918a8ae215645b5a1d7/1628064024328/Group+69.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60">Learning Journeys

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.3s;"><strong>Our students go on Learning Journeys a few times a year which provide rich and meaning experiences outside of the classrooms for them.</strong></p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.307895s;" class="preSlide">Long Service Award Recipients 2022</h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.311842s;">Early childhood educators play a critical role in laying the foundation of learning and holistic development during the golden preschool years - some of the most important years of a child’s life. We honour 14 educators in our family of Methodist preschools who has dedicated the last 5 - 30 years in faithful service to our preschools in our Teachers’ Day Special series. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.315789s;">In this video, our spotlight falls on the 3 award recipients from Sengkang Methodist Preschool (SKMP). Listen to their sharing on what motivates them as teachers and the most fulfilling aspects of their job. Thank you teachers for nurturing every child to be a person of Good Character, who is an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur!</p>

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
